Nicely done Greg!

FYI,
I got a little issue running the dev branch in RHEL 6.6
singularity bootstrap complains about argparse module not found (see below)=
.

I know I am running old OS that contains old python (python-2.6.6-52) but
legacy support is one of the salient feature of Singularity right? :)

Things worked after "sudo -E pip install argparse".  I don't think this was
needed in the previous release... perhaps it should be mentioned in the
release notes... assuming sys admin actually RTFM :-p


Cheers,
Tin
